\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sklearn_2feature__extraction_2text_8py_source_l01495}01495\ \ \ \ \ Tf\ means\ term-\/frequency\ while\ tf-\/idf\ means\ term-\/frequency\ times\ inverse}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sklearn_2feature__extraction_2text_8py_source_l01496}01496\ \ \ \ \ document-\/frequency.\ This\ is\ a\ common\ term\ weighting\ scheme\ in\ information}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sklearn_2feature__extraction_2text_8py_source_l01497}01497\ \ \ \ \ retrieval,\ that\ has\ also\ found\ good\ use\ in\ document\ classification.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sklearn_2feature__extraction_2text_8py_source_l01498}01498\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sklearn_2feature__extraction_2text_8py_source_l01499}01499\ \ \ \ \ The\ goal\ of\ using\ tf-\/idf\ instead\ of\ the\ raw\ frequencies\ of\ occurrence\ of\ a}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sklearn_2feature__extraction_2text_8py_source_l01500}01500\ \ \ \ \ token\ in\ a\ given\ document\ is\ to\ scale\ down\ the\ impact\ of\ tokens\ that\ occur}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sklearn_2feature__extraction_2text_8py_source_l01501}01501\ \ \ \ \ very\ frequently\ in\ a\ given\ corpus\ and\ that\ are\ hence\ empirically\ less}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sklearn_2feature__extraction_2text_8py_source_l01502}01502\ \ \ \ \ informative\ than\ features\ that\ occur\ in\ a\ small\ fraction\ of\ the\ training}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sklearn_2feature__extraction_2text_8py_source_l01503}01503\ \ \ \ \ corpus.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sklearn_2feature__extraction_2text_8py_source_l01504}01504\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sklearn_2feature__extraction_2text_8py_source_l01505}01505\ \ \ \ \ The\ formula\ that\ is\ used\ to\ compute\ the\ tf-\/idf\ for\ a\ term\ t\ of\ a\ document\ d}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sklearn_2feature__extraction_2text_8py_source_l01506}01506\ \ \ \ \ in\ a\ document\ set\ is\ tf-\/idf(t,\ d)\ =\ tf(t,\ d)\ *\ idf(t),\ and\ the\ idf\ is}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sklearn_2feature__extraction_2text_8py_source_l01507}01507\ \ \ \ \ computed\ as\ idf(t)\ =\ log\ [\ n\ /\ df(t)\ ]\ +\ 1\ (if\ \`{}\`{}smooth\_idf=False\`{}\`{}),\ where}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sklearn_2feature__extraction_2text_8py_source_l01508}01508\ \ \ \ \ n\ is\ the\ total\ number\ of\ documents\ in\ the\ document\ set\ and\ df(t)\ is\ the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sklearn_2feature__extraction_2text_8py_source_l01509}01509\ \ \ \ \ document\ frequency\ of\ t;\ the\ document\ frequency\ is\ the\ number\ of\ documents}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sklearn_2feature__extraction_2text_8py_source_l01510}01510\ \ \ \ \ in\ the\ document\ set\ that\ contain\ the\ term\ t.\ The\ effect\ of\ adding\ "{}1"{}\ to}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sklearn_2feature__extraction_2text_8py_source_l01511}01511\ \ \ \ \ the\ idf\ in\ the\ equation\ above\ is\ that\ terms\ with\ zero\ idf,\ i.e.,\ terms}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sklearn_2feature__extraction_2text_8py_source_l01512}01512\ \ \ \ \ that\ occur\ in\ all\ documents\ in\ a\ training\ set,\ will\ not\ be\ entirely}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sklearn_2feature__extraction_2text_8py_source_l01513}01513\ \ \ \ \ ignored.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sklearn_2feature__extraction_2text_8py_source_l01514}01514\ \ \ \ \ (Note\ that\ the\ idf\ formula\ above\ differs\ from\ the\ standard\ textbook}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sklearn_2feature__extraction_2text_8py_source_l01515}01515\ \ \ \ \ notation\ that\ defines\ the\ idf\ as}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sklearn_2feature__extraction_2text_8py_source_l01516}01516\ \ \ \ \ idf(t)\ =\ log\ [\ n\ /\ (df(t)\ +\ 1)\ ]).}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sklearn_2feature__extraction_2text_8py_source_l01517}01517\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sklearn_2feature__extraction_2text_8py_source_l01518}01518\ \ \ \ \ If\ \`{}\`{}smooth\_idf=True\`{}\`{}\ (the\ default),\ the\ constant\ "{}1"{}\ is\ added\ to\ the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sklearn_2feature__extraction_2text_8py_source_l01519}01519\ \ \ \ \ numerator\ and\ denominator\ of\ the\ idf\ as\ if\ an\ extra\ document\ was\ seen}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sklearn_2feature__extraction_2text_8py_source_l01520}01520\ \ \ \ \ containing\ every\ term\ in\ the\ collection\ exactly\ once,\ which\ prevents}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sklearn_2feature__extraction_2text_8py_source_l01521}01521\ \ \ \ \ zero\ divisions:\ idf(t)\ =\ log\ [\ (1\ +\ n)\ /\ (1\ +\ df(t))\ ]\ +\ 1.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sklearn_2feature__extraction_2text_8py_source_l01522}01522\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sklearn_2feature__extraction_2text_8py_source_l01523}01523\ \ \ \ \ Furthermore,\ the\ formulas\ used\ to\ compute\ tf\ and\ idf\ depend}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sklearn_2feature__extraction_2text_8py_source_l01524}01524\ \ \ \ \ on\ parameter\ settings\ that\ correspond\ to\ the\ SMART\ notation\ used\ in\ IR}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sklearn_2feature__extraction_2text_8py_source_l01525}01525\ \ \ \ \ as\ follows:}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{sklearn_2feature__extraction_2text_8py_source_l01527}01527\ \ \ \ \ Tf\ is\ "{}n"{}\ (natural)\ by\ default,\ "{}l"{}\ (logarithmic)\ when}
